This link is broken. The target anchor does not exist or is commented out.
id=sign-up
The anchor after the # symbol points to a non-existent id on the target page. If the anchor link targets the same page nothing will happen when it's clicked. If the anchor link targets another page, then the top of the target page will be displayed instead of the intended location. In most cases the destination anchor has been removed accidentally and should be reinstated.

1101<h4 class="h4">

11022024 James Beard Foundation Book Award Nominees</h4>

1103<p class="p light">

1104Cookbooks and other nonfiction food or beverage-related books that were published in the U.S. in 2023 were eligible to enter the 2024 James Beard Book Awards. Books from foreign publishers must bear a 2023 U.S. copyright date and/or must have been distributed in the U.S. during 2023.</p>

1105<p class="p light">

1106<strong class="strong">

1107Baking and Desserts</strong>

1108<br/>

1109Books with recipes focused on the art and craft of baking, pastries, and desserts, both sweet and savory items, including ingredients, techniques, equipment, and traditions. This year, submissions to the Bread category were included for consideration within the Baking and Desserts category.</p>

1110<p class="p light">

1111<em>

1112Dark Rye and Honey Cake: Festival Baking from Belgium, the Heart of the Low Countries</em>

1113<br/>

1114Regula Ysewijn<br/>

1115(Weldon Owen)</p>

1116<p class="p light">

1117<em>

1118Mayumu: Filipino American Desserts Remixed</em>

1119<br/>

1120Abi Balingit<br/>

1121(HarperCollins)</p>

1122<p class="p light">

1123<em>

1124More Than Cake: 100 Baking Recipes Built for Pleasure and Community</em>

1125<br/>

1126Natasha Pickowicz<br/>

1127(Artisan Books)</p>

1128<p class="p light">

1129<strong class="strong">

1130Beverage with Recipes</strong>

1131<br/>

1132Books with recipes focused on beverages, such as cocktails, beer, wine, spirits, coffee, tea, or juices.</p>

1133<p class="p light">

1134<em>

1135Juke Joints, Jazz Clubs, and Juice: Cocktails from Two Centuries of African American Cookbooks</em>

1136<br/>

1137Toni Tipton-Martin<br/>

1138(Clarkson Potter)</p>

1139<p class="p light">

1140<em>

1141The Maison Premiere Almanac: Cocktails, Oysters, Absinthe, and Other Essential Nutrients for the Sensualist, Aesthete, and Flaneur</em>

1142<br/>

1143Joshua Boissy, Jordan Mackay, and Krystof Zizka with William Elliot<br/>

1144(Clarkson Potter)</p>

1145<p class="p light">

1146<em>

1147Slow Drinks: A Field Guide to Foraging and Fermenting Seasonal Sodas, Botanical Cocktails, Homemade Wines, and More</em>

1148<br/>

1149Danny Childs<br/>

1150(Hardie Grant North America)</p>

1151<p class="p light">

1152<strong class="strong">

1154<br/>

1409<br/>

1410This award is given to either a cookbook that has significantly influenced the way we think about food, honoring authors who possess an exceptional ability to communicate their gastronomic vision via the printed page, or an author whose cookbooks and other culinary books and work, taken together, make a difference in the world of food and cooking. The Book Awards Subcommittee selects the winner for this category. The Cookbook Hall of Fame winner will be announced at the Media Awards ceremony on June 8.</p>

1417<h4 class="h4">

14182024 James Beard Foundation Broadcast Media Award Nominees</h4>

1419<p class="p light">

1420The Broadcast Media Awards recognize non-fiction works in English covering food and beverage topics and appearing widely for the first time in the United States in 2023. These works are from digital and terrestrial media—radio, television broadcasts, podcasts, documentaries, online sites, and social media.<br/>

1636<h4 class="h4">

16372024 James Beard Foundation Journalism Award Nominees</h4>

1638<p class="p light">

1639The Journalism Awards recognize works in English and cover food- or drink-related content which were published—or self-published—in 2023 in any medium.</p>

1640<p class="p light">

1641<strong class="strong">

1642Beverage</strong>

1643<br/>

1644This award recognizes distinctive style, thorough knowledge, plainspoken prose, and innovative approach in a single article on alcoholic or non-alcoholic beverages.</p>

1645<p class="p light">

1646&quot;Bourbon, Biodiversity, and the Quest to Save America&#x27;s Oak Forests&quot;<br/>

1647Betsy Andrews<br/>

1648<em>

1649SevenFifty Daily </em>

1650</p>

1651<p class="p light">

1652&quot;Still Life&quot;<br/>

1653Emily Bingham<br/>

1654<em>

1655Travel + Leisure</em>

1656</p>

1659D. Watkins<br/>

1660<em>

1661Salon </em>

1662</p>

1663<p class="p light">

1664<strong class="strong">

1665Columns and Newsletters</strong>

1666<br/>

1667This award recognizes the work of an individual or team/group that demonstrates thought-provoking opinion and a compelling style on food- or drink-related topics. An entry consists of three examples of a regularly published column or newsletter, in print or online.</p>

1668<p class="p light">

1669&quot;Not from here, not from there&quot;; &quot;Yee-haw!&quot;; &quot;Jajangmyeon&quot;<br/>

1680<p class="p light">

1689<br/>

2083<div class="FooterPartners_partner__tkir8" aria-label=" ">

img elements must have an accessible name.
Add an alt attribute describing the image, which screen readers voice instead of the image. Spacer images and purely decorative images should use alt="" without any global ARIA attributes. Do not use alt text containing only spaces since that's voiced as an unlabeled image.

Impact on users:

  • NVDA 2023.3 Chrome 120 Windows 10 Reading: Image ignored.
  • NVDA 2023.3 FF 115 Windows 10 Reading: Image ignored.
  • NVDA 2023.3 Edge 120 Windows 10 Reading: Image ignored.
  • JAWS 2023.2311.34 Chrome 120 Windows 10 Reading: Image ignored.
  • JAWS 2023.2311.34 FF 115 Windows 10 Reading: Image ignored.
  • JAWS 2023.2311.34 Edge 120 Windows 10 Reading: Image ignored.
  • VoiceOver macOS 13.6 Safari 16.6 macOS 13.6.0 Reading: Image filename read out.
  • VoiceOver iOS 16.6 Safari iOS 16.6 iOS 16.6.1 Touch: Image filename read out, along with OCR text from image.
Line 2084 WCAG 2.2 A F65 Section 508 (2017) A F65
